### Survey reward rules
# gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag = used to prevent stacking deposits

@tier1researchreward_half= 3
@tier1researchmin_half = 30
@tier1researchmax_half = 150

@tier1researchreward_qrt = 1
@tier1researchmin_qrt = 10
@tier1researchmax_qrt = 75

@tier1unityreward_half = 50
@tier1unitymin_half = 50
@tier1unitymax_half = 500


namespace = gpm_survey_minor

# ROOT = ship scope
# FROM = planet scope

############################################################################################################
############################################################################################################
# gpm_hollow_structure
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.1
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.1.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.1.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_hollow_structure
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_hollow_structure }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_hollow_structure_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_hollow_structure_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
		}
		name = DISCONCERTING
		# leader experience
		locked_random_list = {
			90 = {
				LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				LEADER = {	add_trait = leader_trait_paranoid }
				modifier = { factor = 0 LEADER = { has_trait = leader_trait_paranoid } }
			}
		}
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes
						has_deposit = yes
						has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag
					}
				}
			}
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				locked_random_list = {
					16 = { add_deposit = d_physics_2 }
					8 = { add_deposit = d_physics_3 }
					4 = { add_deposit = d_physics_4 }
					2 = { add_deposit = d_physics_5 }
					1 = { add_deposit = d_physics_6 }
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
	#########################
	#### MEGACORP OPTION ####
	#########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_corporate }
		}
		name = gpm_survey.LICENCE_RESEARCH
		# leader experience
		locked_random_list = {
			90 = {
				LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				LEADER = {	add_trait = leader_trait_paranoid }
				modifier = { factor = 0 LEADER = { has_trait = leader_trait_paranoid } }
			}
		}
		# Special Megacorp RP text
		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			locked_random_list = {
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
	########################
	#### MACHINE OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_machine_intelligence }
		}
		name = ACKNOWLEDGED
		# leader experience
		LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes
						has_deposit = yes
						has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag
					}
				}
			}
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
				locked_random_list = {
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 10 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 30 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 70 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 90 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 110 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 120 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 180 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 210 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					3 = { add_resource = { minerals = 290 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					1 = { add_resource = { minerals = 330 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_minerals = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
	#####################
	#### HIVE OPTION ####
	#####################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_hive_mind }
		}
		name = DISTURBING
		# leader experience
		LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes
						has_deposit = yes
						has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag
					}
				}
			}
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
				locked_random_list = {
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 10 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 30 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 70 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 90 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 110 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 120 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 180 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 210 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					3 = { add_resource = { minerals = 290 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					1 = { add_resource = { minerals = 330 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_minerals = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
	#######################
	#### CIVIC OPTIONS ####
	#######################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				OWNER = {
					OR = {
						has_civic = civic_mining_guilds
						has_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
						has_civic = civic_private_prospectors
						owner_species = { has_trait = trait_lithoid }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = DIG
		# leader experience
		LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = no
						has_deposit = no
						NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					}
				}
				gpm_d_random_minerals = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				root.OWNER = { add_resource = { minerals = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
			else = {
				root.OWNER = { add_resource = { minerals = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = gpm_survey.INVESTIGATE.4
		# leader experience
		LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = no
						has_deposit = no
						NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					}
				}
				gpm_d_random_research = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
			else = {
				root.OWNER = {
					add_monthly_resource_mult = {
						resource = physics_research
						value = @tier1researchreward_half
						min = @tier1researchmin_half
						max = @tier1researchmax_half
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				OWNER = {
					OR = {
						has_civic = civic_exalted_priesthood
						has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
						has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = gpm_survey.OMEN
		# leader experience
		LEADER = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = no
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
				gpm_d_random_unity_deposit = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				root.OWNER = { add_resource = { unity = 40 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
			else = {
				root.OWNER = { add_resource = { unity = 110 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# gpm_crystallized_structure
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.5
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.5.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.5.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_crystallized_structure
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_crystallized_structure }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_crystallized_structure_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_crystallized_structure_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = AMAZING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_engineering = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = engineering_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#########################
	#### MEGACORP OPTION ####
	#########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_corporate }
		}
		name = gpm_survey.LICENCE_MINING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# Special Megacorp RP text
		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			locked_random_list = {
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	##############################
	#### RARE CRYSTALS OPTION ####
	##############################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_country_flag = rare_crystals_found }
		}
		name = gpm_survey.CRYSTALS_1
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_crystals = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				locked_random_list = {
					10 = { add_resource = { rare_crystals = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { rare_crystals = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { rare_crystals = 300 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	##############################
	#### MINING GUILDS OPTION ####
	##############################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = {
				OR = {
					has_civic = civic_mining_guilds
					has_civic = civic_machine_rockbreakers
				}
			}
		}
		name = gpm_survey.MINING_GUILDS_1
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_minerals = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				locked_random_list = {
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 10 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 30 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 70 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 90 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 110 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 120 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 180 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 210 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					3 = { add_resource = { minerals = 290 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					1 = { add_resource = { minerals = 330 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# gpm_abandoned_mining_platforms
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.10
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.10.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.10.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_abandoned_mining_platforms
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_abandoned_mining_platforms }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_abandoned_mining_platforms_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_abandoned_mining_platforms_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = CURIOUS
		# leader experience
		locked_random_list = {
			90 = {
				root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_expertise_voidcraft }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_expertise_voidcraft } }
			}
		}
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {

	id = gpm_survey_minor.15
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.15.name"

	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################

	#################

		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_hydrogen_mist }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_hydrogen_mist_discovered } }
	}

	###################

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_salt_flats }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_salt_flats_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_salt_flats_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = INTERESTING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_physics = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half

			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_archaeologist }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_archaeologist } }
			}
		}
		# deposit
		OWNER = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = physics_research
				value = @tier2researchreward
				min = @tier2researchmin
				max = @tier2researchmax
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = engineering_research
				value = @tier2researchreward
				min = @tier2researchmin
				max = @tier2researchmax
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = society_research
				value = @tier2researchreward
				min = @tier2researchmin
				max = @tier2researchmax
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = { gpm_random_minor_artifacts_5 = yes }
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
				locked_random_list = {
					30 = { gpm_random_minor_artifacts_5 = yes }
					10 = {
						add_random_research_option = {
							add_progress = 0.90
							area = engineering
							ignore_prereqs = no
							fail_effects = {
								add_monthly_resource_mult = {
									resource = engineering_research
									value = @tier1researchreward_half
									min = @tier1researchmin_half
									max = @tier1researchmax_half
								}
							}
						}
					}
					10 = {
						add_random_research_option = {
							add_progress = 0.90
							area = physics
							ignore_prereqs = no
							fail_effects = {
								add_monthly_resource_mult = {
									resource = physics_research
									value = @tier1researchreward_half
									min = @tier1researchmin_half
									max = @tier1researchmax_half
								}
							}
						}
					}
					10 = {

							add_progress = 0.90
							area = society
							ignore_prereqs = no
							fail_effects = {
								add_monthly_resource_mult = {
									resource = society_research
									value = @tier1researchreward_half
									min = @tier1researchmin_half
									max = @tier1researchmax_half
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}

# gpm_water_pockets
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.30
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.30.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.30.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_water_pockets
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_water_pockets }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_water_pockets_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_water_pockets_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = ASTOUNDING
		# leader experience
		locked_random_list = {
			90 = {
				root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds } }
			}
		}
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_society = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = society_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#########################
	#### MEGACORP OPTION ####
	#########################

		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_corporate }
		}

				root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds } }
			}
		}
		# Special Megacorp RP text
		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp

		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			locked_random_list = {
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }

# gpm_viscous_gas_layer
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.45
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.45.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.45.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_viscous_gas_layer
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_viscous_gas_layer }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_viscous_gas_layer_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_viscous_gas_layer_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = DISCONCERTING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_physics = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.50.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_everlasting_tornadoes
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_everlasting_tornadoes }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_everlasting_tornadoes_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_everlasting_tornadoes_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = INTRIGUING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_physics = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}

# gpm_super_heated_atmosphere
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.75
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.75.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.75.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_super_heated_atmosphere
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_super_heated_atmosphere }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_super_heated_atmosphere_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_super_heated_atmosphere_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = PECULIAR
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_engineering = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = engineering_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#########################
	#### MEGACORP OPTION ####
	#########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_corporate }
		}
		name = gpm_survey.LICENCE_RESEARCH_2
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# Special Megacorp RP text
		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			locked_random_list = {
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }

# gpm_proto_planet
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.100
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.100.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.100.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_proto_planet
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_proto_planet }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_proto_planet_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_proto_planet_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = FASCINATING
		# leader experience
		locked_random_list = {
			90 = {
				root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds } }
			}
		}
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_physics = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = physics_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#########################
	#### MEGACORP OPTION ####
	#########################
	option = {

			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_corporate }
		}

				root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_expertise_new_worlds } }
			}
		}
		# Special Megacorp RP text
		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }

		}
		# other rewards

		trigger = { }

			limit = {

						has_deposit = no

							has_deposit = yes

		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			locked_random_list = {
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#############################
	#### MATERIALISTS OPTION ####
	#############################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = {
				OR = {
					has_ethic = ethic_materialist
					has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				}
			}
		}
		name = gpm_survey.RESEARCH_EMPIRE_7
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					has_deposit = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_ancrel = yes }
					add_deposit = d_artifacts_1
					gpm_d_random_unity_deposit_big = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_ancrel = no }
					add_deposit = gpm_d_triple_science
					gpm_d_random_unity_deposit_big = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				locked_random_list = {
					20 = {
						add_monthly_resource_mult = {
							resource = unity
							value = 8
							min = 40
							max = 200
						}
					}
					10 = {
						add_monthly_resource_mult = {
							resource = unity
							value = 16
							min = 80
							max = 400
						}
					}
					5 = {
						add_monthly_resource_mult = {
							resource = unity
							value = 32
							min = 150
							max = 750
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = physics_research
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = society_research
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax
			}
			add_monthly_resource_mult = {
				resource = engineering_research
				value = @tier1researchreward
				min = @tier1researchmin
				max = @tier1researchmax
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# gpm_lingering_pollution
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.140
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.140.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.140.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_lingering_pollution
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_lingering_pollution }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_lingering_pollution_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_lingering_pollution_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = INTRIGUING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					NOT = { gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_society = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				add_monthly_resource_mult = {
					resource = society_research
					value = @tier1researchreward_half
					min = @tier1researchmin_half
					max = @tier1researchmax_half
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#########################
	#### MEGACORP OPTION ####
	#########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = { has_authority = auth_corporate }
		}
		name = gpm_survey.LICENCE_RESEARCH
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# Special Megacorp RP text
		custom_tooltip = gpm_survey_reward_deposit_megacorp
		# deposit
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					NOT = { gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes }
				}
				gpm_d_random_trade = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			locked_random_list = {
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				10 = { add_resource = { energy = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				9 = { add_resource = { energy = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				7 = { add_resource = { energy = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				6 = { add_resource = { energy = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				5 = { add_resource = { energy = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
			}
		}

			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }

			}

			}
			10 = {
				root.leader = {	add_trait = leader_trait_xeno_cataloger }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_xeno_cataloger } }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.owner = { is_machine_empire = no } }
			}
			10 = {

				modifier = { factor = 0 root.leader = {	has_trait = leader_trait_roamer } }
				modifier = { factor = 0 root.owner = { is_gestalt = yes } }
			}
		}
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {

					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no

							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_unity_deposit = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}

				gpm_random_unity = yes
			}

				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes

	#################

		FROM = { has_modifier = gpm_heavy_metal_coral }
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_heavy_metal_coral_discovered } }
	}

	###################

						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station
						}
					}

			}

				gpm_d_random_minerals_med = yes

					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_unity_deposit = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				gpm_random_unity = yes
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	###########################
	#### REANIMATOR OPTION ####
	###########################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = {
				has_civic = civic_reanimated_armies
			}
		}
		name = gpm_survey.REANIMATOR
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_unity_deposit = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				gpm_random_unity = yes
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		OWNER = {
			random_list = {
				10 = {
					create_fleet = {
						name = "NAME_Reanimated_Leviathan"
						effect = {
							set_owner = root
							create_ship = {
								name = "NAME_Grand_Father"
								design = "NAME_Shard_Dragon"
								prefix = no
								upgradable = no
								effect = {
									add_modifier = { modifier = gpm_ship_balancer_leviathan }
								}
							}
							set_location = {
								target = from
								distance = 0
								angle = random
							}
							set_fleet_stance = passive
						}
						settings = {
							can_upgrade = no
							can_change_composition = no
							can_change_leader = no
							uses_naval_capacity = no
							spawn_debris = no
						}
					}
				}
				10 = {
					add_monthly_resource_mult = {
						resource = society_research
						value = @tier3researchreward
						min = @tier3researchmin
						max = @tier3researchmax
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# gpm_toxic_garbage or gpm_garbage_dump
ship_event = {
	id = gpm_survey_minor.165
	title = "gpm_survey_minor.165.name"
	desc = "gpm_survey_minor.165.desc"
	picture = GFX_evt_gpm_toxic_garbage
	show_sound = event_scanner
	location = FROM

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#################
	#### TRIGGER ####
	#################
	trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_modifier = gpm_toxic_garbage
				has_modifier = gpm_garbage_dump
			}
		}
		OWNER = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gpm_toxic_garbage_discovered } }
	}

	###################
	#### IMMEDIATE ####
	###################
	immediate = {
		OWNER = { set_country_flag = gpm_toxic_garbage_discovered }
	}

	########################
	#### DEFAULT OPTION ####
	########################
	option = {
		trigger = { }
		name = DISCONCERTING
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					NOT = { gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_minerals = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				locked_random_list = {
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 10 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 30 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 70 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 90 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 110 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 120 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 180 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 210 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }

							has_communications = root.owner
						}

							type = GPM_MESSAGE_RELIC_POSSESSION

								type = name

							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = gpm_r_machine_world_core_found
				modifier = { factor = 0 has_global_flag = gpm_relic_drops_disabled }

		locked_random_list = {
			90 = { }
			10 = {
				root.owner = {
					add_relic = gpm_r_machine_world_core
					log = "<< RELICS >> | ADD_RELIC <<< gpm_r_machine_world_core >>> to ROOT.OWNER = [root.owner.GetName] ; survey event reward"
					every_relation = {
						limit = {
							gpm_is_country_type_default = yes
							has_communications = root.owner
						}
						log = "<< RELICS >> | RELIC LOOTED <<< create message on THIS = [THIS.GetName]; every relation notifcation"
						create_message = {
							type = GPM_MESSAGE_RELIC_POSSESSION
							localization = GPM_MESSAGE_RELIC_POSSESSION_DESC
							days = 30
							target = root.owner.capital_scope
							variable = {
								type = name
								localization = COUNTRY
								scope = root.owner
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = gpm_r_machine_world_core_found
				modifier = { factor = 0 has_global_flag = gpm_relic_drops_disabled }
				modifier = { factor = 0
					root.owner = {
						OR = {
							has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}

	###############################
	#### INDUSTRIALISTS OPTION ####
	###############################
	option = {
		trigger = {
			OWNER = {
				is_relentless_industrialist_empire = yes
			}
		}
		name = gpm_survey.INDUSTRIALIST_5
		# leader experience
		root.leader = { gpm_random_experience = yes }
		# deposit
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					NOT = { has_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
					NOT = { gpm_is_planet_class_normal_habitable = yes }
					OR = {
						has_deposit = no
						AND = {
							has_deposit = yes
							has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				gpm_d_random_minerals = yes
				gpm_d_random_alloys = yes
				hidden_effect = { set_planet_flag = gpm_has_been_deposit_explored_flag }
			}
		}
		else = {
			OWNER = {
				locked_random_list = {
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 5 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 25 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 50 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 75 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 100 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 125 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					10 = { add_resource = { minerals = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 150 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					9 = { add_resource = { minerals = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 175 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					7 = { add_resource = { minerals = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 200 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					6 = { add_resource = { minerals = 275 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 225 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
					5 = { add_resource = { minerals = 300 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } add_resource = { alloys = 250 multiplier = value:gpm_leader_level_value } }
				}
			}
		}
		# other rewards
		locked_random_list = {
			90 = { }
			10 = {
				root.owner = {
					add_relic = gpm_r_machine_world_core
					log = "<< RELICS >> | ADD_RELIC <<< gpm_r_machine_world_core >>> to ROOT.OWNER = [root.owner.GetName] ; survey event reward"
					every_relation = {
						limit = {
							gpm_is_country_type_default = yes
							has_communications = root.owner
						}
						log = "<< RELICS >> | RELIC LOOTED <<< create message on THIS = [THIS.GetName]; every relation notifcation"
						create_message = {
							type = GPM_MESSAGE_RELIC_POSSESSION
							localization = GPM_MESSAGE_RELIC_POSSESSION_DESC
							days = 30
							target = root.owner.capital_scope
							variable = {
								type = name
								localization = COUNTRY
								scope = root.owner
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = gpm_r_machine_world_core_found
				modifier = { factor = 0 has_global_flag = gpm_relic_drops_disabled }
				modifier = { factor = 0
					root.owner = {
						OR = {
							has_ethic = ethic_spiritualist
							has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		# bonus rewards
		OWNER = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_policy_flag = gpm_more_discovery_rewards }
				gpm_exploration_policy_away_teams_reward = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
